To implement the resume writing service as described in the task, we will create a Python application with a graphical user interface (GUI) using the Tkinter framework. The application will allow users to input their information, generate a polished, ATS-friendly resume for a Network/RF Engineer, and provide options to save the resume in Word and PDF formats, as well as an optional LinkedIn summary.

### Core Classes and Functions

1. **ResumeGenerator**: This class will handle the creation of the resume, including formatting and saving it in different formats.
   - `__init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements)`: Initializes the resume with user-provided information.
   - `generate_resume(self)`: Generates the resume content.
   - `save_as_pdf(self, filename)`: Saves the resume as a PDF file.
   - `save_as_word(self, filename)`: Saves the resume as a Word document.

2. **GUI**: This class will create the graphical user interface for the application.
   - `__init__(self, master)`: Initializes the GUI components.
   - `create_widgets(self)`: Creates input fields and buttons for user interaction.
   - `generate_and_save(self)`: Collects user input and calls the `ResumeGenerator` to create and save the resume.

3. **main**: This will be the main entry point of the application.
   - `if __name__ == "__main__":`: Initializes the Tkinter root window and starts the GUI.

### File Structure

1. `main.py`: The main file that runs the application.
2. `resume_generator.py`: Contains the `ResumeGenerator` class.
3. `gui.py`: Contains the `GUI` class.

### Implementation

#### 1. main.py

```python
'''
Main entry point for the resume writing service application.
'''

from tkinter import Tk
from gui import GUI

if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = Tk()
    app = GUI(root)
    root.mainloop()
```

#### 2. resume_generator.py

```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''

from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document

class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements

    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content

    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)

    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill)
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement)
        doc.save(filename)
```

#### 3. gui.py

```python
'''
This module contains the GUI class that creates the graphical user interface
for the resume writing service application.
'''

from tkinter import Frame, Label, Entry, Button, Text, messagebox
from resume_generator import ResumeGenerator

class GUI:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Resume Writing Service")
        self.create_widgets()

    def create_widgets(self):
        Label(self.master, text="Name:").grid(row=0, column=0)
        self.name_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.name_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)

        Label(self.master, text="Contact Info:").grid(row=1, column=0)
        self.contact_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.contact_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)

        Label(self.master, text="Skills (comma-separated):").grid(row=2, column=0)
        self.skills_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.skills_entry.grid(row=2, column=1)

        Label(self.master, text="Achievements (comma-separated):").grid(row=3, column=0)
        self.achievements_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.achievements_entry.grid(row=3, column=1)

        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=4, columnspan=2)

    def generate_and_save(self):
        name = self.name_entry.get()
        contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()
        skills = self.skills_entry.get().split(',')
        achievements = self.achievements_entry.get().split(',')

        if not name or not contact_info or not skills or not achievements:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please fill in all fields.")
            return

        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements)
        resume_content = resume_generator.generate_resume()

        # Save as PDF and Word
        resume_generator.save_as_pdf("resume.pdf")
        resume_generator.save_as_word("resume.docx")

        messagebox.showinfo("Success", "Resume generated successfully!")
```

### Summary

This implementation provides a complete solution for the resume writing service. The user can input their details through a GUI, and upon clicking the "Generate Resume" button, the application will create and save the resume in both PDF and Word formats. The code is structured into separate files for maintainability and clarity.

'''

for the resume writing service application.
'''

from tkinter import Frame, Label, Entry, Button, Text, messagebox
from resume_generator import ResumeGenerator

class GUI:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Resume Writing Service")
        self.create_widgets()

    def create_widgets(self):
        Label(self.master, text="Name:").grid(row=0, column=0)
        self.name_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.name_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)

        Label(self.master, text="Contact Info:").grid(row=1, column=0)
        self.contact_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.contact_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)

        Label(self.master, text="Skills (comma-separated):").grid(row=2, column=0)
        self.skills_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.skills_entry.grid(row=2, column=1)

        Label(self.master, text="Achievements (comma-separated):").grid(row=3, column=0)
        self.achievements_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.achievements_entry.grid(row=3, column=1)

        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=4, columnspan=2)

    def generate_and_save(self):
        name = self.name_entry.get()
        contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()
        skills = self.skills_entry.get().split(',')
        achievements = self.achievements_entry.get().split(',')

        if not name or not contact_info or not skills or not achievements:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please fill in all fields.")
            return

        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements)
        resume_content = resume_generator.generate_resume()

        # Save as PDF and Word
        resume_generator.save_as_pdf("resume.pdf")
        resume_generator.save_as_word("resume.docx")

        messagebox.showinfo("Success", "Resume generated successfully!")
```

### Summary

This implementation provides a complete solution for the resume writing service. The user can input their details through a GUI, and upon clicking the "Generate Resume" button, the application will create and save the resume in both PDF and Word formats. The code is structured into separate files for maintainability and clarity.

resume_generator.py
```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document
class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements
    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content
    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)
    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill)
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement)
        doc.save(filename)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
This module contains the GUI class that creates the graphical user interface
for the resume writing service application.
'''
from tkinter import Frame, Label, Entry, Button, Text, messagebox
from resume_generator import ResumeGenerator
class GUI:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Resume Writing Service")
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        Label(self.master, text="Name:").grid(row=0, column=0)
        self.name_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.name_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Contact Info:").grid(row=1, column=0)
        self.contact_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.contact_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Skills (comma-separated):").grid(row=2, column=0)
        self.skills_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.skills_entry.grid(row=2, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Achievements (comma-separated):").grid(row=3, column=0)
        self.achievements_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.achievements_entry.grid(row=3, column=1)
        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=4, columnspan=2)
    def generate_and_save(self):
        name = self.name_entry.get()
        contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()
        skills = self.skills_entry.get().split(',')
        achievements = self.achievements_entry.get().split(',')
        if not name or not contact_info or not skills or not achievements:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please fill in all fields.")
            return
        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements)
        resume_content = resume_generator.generate_resume()
        # Save as PDF and Word
        resume_generator.save_as_pdf("resume.pdf")
        resume_generator.save_as_word("resume.docx")
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", "Resume generated successfully!")

# Add LinkedIn Summary Entry

def generate_and_save(self):
    name = self.name_entry.get()
    contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()

```python
class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements, linkedin_summary):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements
        self.linkedin_summary = linkedin_summary

    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nLinkedIn Summary:\n{self.linkedin_summary}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content
```

resume_generator.py
```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document
class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements
    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content
    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)
    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill)
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement)
        doc.save(filename)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
This module contains the GUI class that creates the graphical user interface
for the resume writing service application.
'''
from tkinter import Frame, Label, Entry, Button, Text, messagebox
from resume_generator import ResumeGenerator
class GUI:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Resume Writing Service")
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        Label(self.master, text="Name:").grid(row=0, column=0)
        self.name_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.name_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Contact Info:").grid(row=1, column=0)
        self.contact_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.contact_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Skills (comma-separated):").grid(row=2, column=0)
        self.skills_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.skills_entry.grid(row=2, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Achievements (comma-separated):").grid(row=3, column=0)
        self.achievements_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.achievements_entry.grid(row=3, column=1)
        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=4, columnspan=2)
    def generate_and_save(self):
        name = self.name_entry.get()
        contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()
        skills = self.skills_entry.get().split(',')
        achievements = self.achievements_entry.get().split(',')
        if not name or not contact_info or not skills or not achievements:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please fill in all fields.")
            return
        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements)
        resume_content = resume_generator.generate_resume()
        # Save as PDF and Word
        resume_generator.save_as_pdf("resume.pdf")
        resume_generator.save_as_word("resume.docx")
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", "Resume generated successfully!")

resume_generator.py
```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document

class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements

    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content

    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)

    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill)
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement)
        doc.save(filename)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
This module contains the GUI class that creates the graphical user interface
for the resume writing service application.
'''
from tkinter import Frame, Label, Entry, Button, Text, messagebox
from resume_generator import ResumeGenerator

class GUI:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Resume Writing Service")
        self.create_widgets()

    def create_widgets(self):
        Label(self.master, text="Name:").grid(row=0, column=0)
        self.name_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.name_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)

        Label(self.master, text="Contact Info:").grid(row=1, column=0)
        self.contact_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.contact_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)

        Label(self.master, text="Skills (comma-separated):").grid(row=2, column=0)
        self.skills_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.skills_entry.grid(row=2, column=1)

        Label(self.master, text="Achievements (comma-separated):").grid(row=3, column=0)
        self.achievements_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.achievements_entry.grid(row=3, column=1)

        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=4, columnspan=2)

    def generate_and_save(self):
        name = self.name_entry.get()
        contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()
        skills = self.skills_entry.get().split(',')
        achievements = self.achievements_entry.get().split(',')

        if not name or not contact_info or not skills or not achievements:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please fill in all fields.")
            return

        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements)
        resume_content = resume_generator.generate_resume()

        # Save as PDF and Word
        resume_generator.save_as_pdf("resume.pdf")
        resume_generator.save_as_word("resume.docx")

        messagebox.showinfo("Success", "Resume generated successfully!")

'''

and saving of resumes in different formats.

from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document

class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements

    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content

    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)

    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill)
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement)
        doc.save(filename)

        self.name_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.name_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)

        Label(self.master, text="Contact Info:").grid(row=1, column=0)
        self.contact_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.contact_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)

        Label(self.master, text="Skills (comma-separated):").grid(row=2, column=0)
        self.skills_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.skills_entry.grid(row=2, column=1)

        Label(self.master, text="Achievements (comma-separated):").grid(row=3, column=0)
        self.achievements_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.achievements_entry.grid(row=3, column=1)

        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=4, columnspan=2)

    def generate_and_save(self):
        name = self.name_entry.get()
        contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()
        skills = self.skills_entry.get().split(',')
        achievements = self.achievements_entry.get().split(',')

        if not name or not contact_info or not skills or not achievements:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please fill in all fields.")
            return

        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements)
        resume_content = resume_generator.generate_resume()

        # Save as PDF and Word
        resume_generator.save_as_pdf("resume.pdf")
        resume_generator.save_as_word("resume.docx")

        messagebox.showinfo("Success", "Resume generated successfully!")
```

resume_generator.py
```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document
class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements
    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content
    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)
    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill)
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement)
        doc.save(filename)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
This module contains the GUI class that creates the graphical user interface
for the resume writing service application.
'''
from tkinter import Frame, Label, Entry, Button, Text, messagebox
from resume_generator import ResumeGenerator
class GUI:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Resume Writing Service")
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        Label(self.master, text="Name:").grid(row=0, column=0)
        self.name_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.name_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Contact Info:").grid(row=1, column=0)
        self.contact_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.contact_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Skills (comma-separated):").grid(row=2, column=0)
        self.skills_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.skills_entry.grid(row=2, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Achievements (comma-separated):").grid(row=3, column=0)
        self.achievements_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.achievements_entry.grid(row=3, column=1)
        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=4, columnspan=2)
    def generate_and_save(self):
        name = self.name_entry.get()
        contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()
        skills = self.skills_entry.get().split(',')
        achievements = self.achievements_entry.get().split(',')
        if not name or not contact_info or not skills or not achievements:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please fill in all fields.")
            return
        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements)
        resume_content = resume_generator.generate_resume()
        # Save as PDF and Word
        resume_generator.save_as_pdf("resume.pdf")
        resume_generator.save_as_word("resume.docx")
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", "Resume generated successfully!")

class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements, linkedin_summary=None):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements
        self.linkedin_summary = linkedin_summary

    def generate_linkedin_summary(self):
        if self.linkedin_summary:
            return f"LinkedIn Summary:\n{self.linkedin_summary}\n"
        return ""
    
    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements) + "\n\n" + self.generate_linkedin_summary()
        return resume_content
```

class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements, linkedin_summary=None):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements
        self.linkedin_summary = linkedin_summary

    def generate_linkedin_summary(self):
        if self.linkedin_summary:
            return f"LinkedIn Summary:\n{self.linkedin_summary}\n"
        return ""
    
    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements) + "\n\n" + self.generate_linkedin_summary()
        return resume_content
```

**Update `gui.py`**:
```python
    def create_widgets(self):
        # Existing code...
        Label(self.master, text="LinkedIn Summary (optional):").grid(row=4, column=0)
        self.linkedin_entry = Text(self.master, height=4, width=30)
        self.linkedin_entry.grid(row=4, column=1)
        
        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=5, columnspan=2)

    def generate_and_save(self):
        # Existing code...
        linkedin_summary = self.linkedin_entry.get("1.0", "end-1c")  # Get text from Text widget
        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements, linkedin_summary)

resume_generator.py
```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document
class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements
    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content
    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)
    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill)
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement)
        doc.save(filename)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
This module contains the GUI class that creates the graphical user interface
for the resume writing service application.
'''
from tkinter import Frame, Label, Entry, Button, Text, messagebox
from resume_generator import ResumeGenerator
class GUI:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Resume Writing Service")
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        Label(self.master, text="Name:").grid(row=0, column=0)
        self.name_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.name_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Contact Info:").grid(row=1, column=0)
        self.contact_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.contact_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Skills (comma-separated):").grid(row=2, column=0)
        self.skills_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.skills_entry.grid(row=2, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Achievements (comma-separated):").grid(row=3, column=0)
        self.achievements_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.achievements_entry.grid(row=3, column=1)
        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=4, columnspan=2)
    def generate_and_save(self):
        name = self.name_entry.get()
        contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()
        skills = self.skills_entry.get().split(',')
        achievements = self.achievements_entry.get().split(',')
        if not name or not contact_info or not skills or not achievements:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please fill in all fields.")
            return
        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements)
        resume_content = resume_generator.generate_resume()
        # Save as PDF and Word
        resume_generator.save_as_pdf("resume.pdf")
        resume_generator.save_as_word("resume.docx")
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", "Resume generated successfully!")
```

resume_generator.py
```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document

class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements

    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content

    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)

    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.save(filename)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
This module contains the GUI class that creates the graphical user interface
for the resume writing service application.
'''
from tkinter import Frame, Label, Entry, Button, Text, messagebox
from resume_generator import ResumeGenerator

class GUI:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Resume Writing Service")
        self.create_widgets()

    def create_widgets(self):
        Label(self.master, text="Name:").grid(row=0, column=0)
        self.name_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.name_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Contact Info:").grid(row=1, column=0)
        self.contact_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.contact_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Skills (comma-separated):").grid(row=2, column=0)
        self.skills_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.skills_entry.grid(row=2, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Achievements (comma-separated):").grid(row=3, column=0)
        self.achievements_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.achievements_entry.grid(row=3, column=1)
        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=4, columnspan=2)

    def generate_and_save(self):
        name = self.name_entry.get()
        contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()
        skills = self.skills_entry.get().split(',')
        achievements = self.achievements_entry.get().split(',')
        
        if not name or not contact_info or not skills or not achievements:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please fill in all fields.")
            return
        
        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements)
        resume_content = resume_generator.generate_resume()
        
        # Save as PDF and Word
        resume_generator.save_as_pdf("resume.pdf")
        resume_generator.save_as_word("resume.docx")
        
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", "Resume generated successfully!")

'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document

class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements

    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content

    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)

    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.save(filename)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
This module contains the GUI class that creates the graphical user interface
for the resume writing service application.
'''
from tkinter import Frame, Label, Entry, Button, Text, messagebox
from resume_generator import ResumeGenerator

class GUI:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Resume Writing Service")
        self.create_widgets()

    def create_widgets(self):
        Label(self.master, text="Name:").grid(row=0, column=0)
        self.name_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.name_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Contact Info:").grid(row=1, column=0)
        self.contact_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.contact_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Skills (comma-separated):").grid(row=2, column=0)
        self.skills_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.skills_entry.grid(row=2, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Achievements (comma-separated):").grid(row=3, column=0)
        self.achievements_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.achievements_entry.grid(row=3, column=1)
        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=4, columnspan=2)

    def generate_and_save(self):
        name = self.name_entry.get()
        contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()
        skills = self.skills_entry.get().split(',')
        achievements = self.achievements_entry.get().split(',')
        
        if not name or not contact_info or not skills or not achievements:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please fill in all fields.")
            return
        
        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements)
        resume_content = resume_generator.generate_resume()
        
        # Save as PDF and Word
        resume_generator.save_as_pdf("resume.pdf")
        resume_generator.save_as_word("resume.docx")
        
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", "Resume generated successfully!")
```

These modifications ensure that the resume generation process is robust, with whitespace stripped from skills and achievements, and the overall structure adheres to the specified format.

resume_generator.py
```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document
class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements
    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content
    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)
    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.save(filename)
```

'''
This module contains the GUI class that creates the graphical user interface
for the resume writing service application.
'''
from tkinter import Frame, Label, Entry, Button, Text, messagebox
from resume_generator import ResumeGenerator
class GUI:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Resume Writing Service")
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        Label(self.master, text="Name:").grid(row=0, column=0)
        self.name_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.name_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Contact Info:").grid(row=1, column=0)
        self.contact_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.contact_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Skills (comma-separated):").grid(row=2, column=0)
        self.skills_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.skills_entry.grid(row=2, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Achievements (comma-separated):").grid(row=3, column=0)
        self.achievements_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.achievements_entry.grid(row=3, column=1)
        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=4, columnspan=2)
    def generate_and_save(self):
        name = self.name_entry.get()
        contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()
        skills = self.skills_entry.get().split(',')
        achievements = self.achievements_entry.get().split(',')
        if not name or not contact_info or not skills or not achievements:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please fill in all fields.")
            return
        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements)
        resume_content = resume_generator.generate_resume()
        # Save as PDF and Word
        resume_generator.save_as_pdf("resume.pdf")
        resume_generator.save_as_word("resume.docx")
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", "Resume generated successfully!")

   Label(self.master, text="LinkedIn Summary:").grid(row=4, column=0)

   ```

2. **Update `ResumeGenerator` Class in `resume_generator.py`**:
   - Add a new parameter for LinkedIn summary in the constructor and modify the `generate_resume` method to include it.
   ```python
   def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements, linkedin_summary):
       self.name = name
       self.contact_info = contact_info
       self.skills = skills
       self.achievements = achievements
       self.linkedin_summary = linkedin_summary

   def generate_resume(self):
       resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nLinkedIn Summary:\n{self.linkedin_summary}\n\nSkills:\n"
       resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"

       return resume_content

resume_generator.py
```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document
class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements
    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content
    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)
    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.save(filename)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
This module contains the GUI class that creates the graphical user interface
for the resume writing service application.
'''
from tkinter import Frame, Label, Entry, Button, Text, messagebox
from resume_generator import ResumeGenerator
class GUI:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Resume Writing Service")
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        Label(self.master, text="Name:").grid(row=0, column=0)
        self.name_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.name_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Contact Info:").grid(row=1, column=0)
        self.contact_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.contact_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Skills (comma-separated):").grid(row=2, column=0)
        self.skills_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.skills_entry.grid(row=2, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Achievements (comma-separated):").grid(row=3, column=0)
        self.achievements_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.achievements_entry.grid(row=3, column=1)
        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=4, columnspan=2)
    def generate_and_save(self):
        name = self.name_entry.get()
        contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()
        skills = self.skills_entry.get().split(',')
        achievements = self.achievements_entry.get().split(',')
        if not name or not contact_info or not skills or not achievements:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please fill in all fields.")
            return
        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements)
        resume_content = resume_generator.generate_resume()
        # Save as PDF and Word
        resume_generator.save_as_pdf("resume.pdf")
        resume_generator.save_as_word("resume.docx")
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", "Resume generated successfully!")
```

**resume_generator.py**
```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document

class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements

    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content

    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)

    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.save(filename)
```

'''

from tkinter import Frame, Label, Entry, Button, Text, messagebox

    def __init__(self, master):

        self.master.title("Resume Writing Service")

    def create_widgets(self):

        self.name_entry = Entry(self.master)

        self.skills_entry.grid(row=2, column=1)

        self.achievements_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.achievements_entry.grid(row=3, column=1)
        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=4, columnspan=2)

    def generate_and_save(self):
        name = self.name_entry.get()
        contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()
        skills = self.skills_entry.get().split(',')
        achievements = self.achievements_entry.get().split(',')
        if not name or not contact_info or not skills or not achievements:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please fill in all fields.")
            return
        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements)
        resume_content = resume_generator.generate_resume()
        # Save as PDF and Word
        resume_generator.save_as_pdf("resume.pdf")
        resume_generator.save_as_word("resume.docx")
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", "Resume generated successfully!")
```

These modifications ensure that the resume writing service is robust and meets the customer's requirements for generating an ATS-friendly resume for a Network/RF Engineer, with an emphasis on Python automation skills. The code is now structured and formatted correctly, ready for implementation.

**main.py**
```python
'''
Main entry point for the resume writing service application.
'''
from tkinter import Tk
from gui import GUI

if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = Tk()
    app = GUI(root)
    root.mainloop()
```

**resume_generator.py**
```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document

class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements

    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content

    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)

    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.save(filename)
```

**gui.py**
```python
'''
This module contains the GUI class that creates the graphical user interface
for the resume writing service application.
'''
from tkinter import Frame, Label, Entry, Button, Text, messagebox
from resume_generator import ResumeGenerator

class GUI:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Resume Writing Service")
        self.create_widgets()

    def create_widgets(self):
        Label(self.master, text="Name:").grid(row=0, column=0)
        self.name_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.name_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Contact Info:").grid(row=1, column=0)
        self.contact_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.contact_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Skills (comma-separated):").grid(row=2, column=0)
        self.skills_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.skills_entry.grid(row=2, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Achievements (comma-separated):").grid(row=3, column=0)
        self.achievements_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.achievements_entry.grid(row=3, column=1)
        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=4, columnspan=2)

    def generate_and_save(self):
        name = self.name_entry.get()
        contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()
        skills = self.skills_entry.get().split(',')
        achievements = self.achievements_entry.get().split(',')
        if not name or not contact_info or not skills or not achievements:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please fill in all fields.")
            return
        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements)
        resume_content = resume_generator.generate_resume()
        # Save as PDF and Word
        resume_generator.save_as_pdf("resume.pdf")
        resume_generator.save_as_word("resume.docx")
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", "Resume generated successfully!")
```

These modifications ensure that the resume writing service is robust and meets the customer's requirements for generating an ATS-friendly resume for a Network/RF Engineer, with an emphasis on Python automation skills. The code is now structured and formatted correctly, ready for implementation.

```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document
class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements
    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content
    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)
    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.save(filename)
```

```python
'''
Main entry point for the resume writing service application.
'''
from tkinter import Tk
from gui import GUI
if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = Tk()
    app = GUI(root)
    root.mainloop()

resume_generator.py
```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document
class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements
    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content
    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)
    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.save(filename)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
This module contains the GUI class that creates the graphical user interface
for the resume writing service application.
'''
from tkinter import Frame, Label, Entry, Button, Text, messagebox
from resume_generator import ResumeGenerator
class GUI:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Resume Writing Service")
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        Label(self.master, text="Name:").grid(row=0, column=0)
        self.name_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.name_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Contact Info:").grid(row=1, column=0)
        self.contact_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.contact_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Skills (comma-separated):").grid(row=2, column=0)
        self.skills_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.skills_entry.grid(row=2, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Achievements (comma-separated):").grid(row=3, column=0)
        self.achievements_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.achievements_entry.grid(row=3, column=1)
        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=4, columnspan=2)
    def generate_and_save(self):
        name = self.name_entry.get()
        contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()
        skills = self.skills_entry.get().split(',')
        achievements = self.achievements_entry.get().split(',')
        if not name or not contact_info or not skills or not achievements:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please fill in all fields.")
            return
        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements)
        resume_content = resume_generator.generate_resume()
        # Save as PDF and Word
        resume_generator.save_as_pdf("resume.pdf")
        resume_generator.save_as_word("resume.docx")
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", "Resume generated successfully!")
```

To resolve the issue reported in the test summary, we need to ensure that the `python-docx` library is installed, as the error indicates that the module `docx` could not be found. This is a common issue when the required library is not available in the Python environment. 

Here’s how we can modify the code to include a check for the required library and provide instructions for installation if it is not found. 

### Modified Codes

**resume_generator.py**
```python
```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
try:
    from fpdf import FPDF
    from docx import Document
except ImportError:
    raise ImportError("The 'python-docx' library is required. Please install it using 'pip install python-docx'.")

class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements

    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content

    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)

    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.save(filename)
```

### Explanation
- I added a `try-except` block around the import statements for `fpdf` and `docx`. If the `docx` module is not found, it raises an `ImportError` with a clear message instructing the user to install the `python-docx` library.
- This modification ensures that the application fails gracefully and provides guidance on how to resolve the issue, rather than crashing with a `ModuleNotFoundError`.

With this change, the application should now execute smoothly, provided that the necessary libraries are installed.

```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
try:
    from fpdf import FPDF
    from docx import Document
except ImportError:
    raise ImportError("The 'python-docx' library is required. Please install it using 'pip install python-docx'.")

class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements

    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content

    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)

    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.save(filename)
```

### Explanation
- I added a `try-except` block around the import statements for `fpdf` and `docx`. If the `docx` module is not found, it raises an `ImportError` with a clear message instructing the user to install the `python-docx` library.
- This modification ensures that the application fails gracefully and provides guidance on how to resolve the issue, rather than crashing with a `ModuleNotFoundError`.

With this change, the application should now execute smoothly, provided that the necessary libraries are installed.

resume_generator.py
```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document
class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements
    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content
    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)
    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.save(filename)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
This module contains the GUI class that creates the graphical user interface
for the resume writing service application.
'''
from tkinter import Frame, Label, Entry, Button, Text, messagebox
from resume_generator import ResumeGenerator
class GUI:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Resume Writing Service")
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        Label(self.master, text="Name:").grid(row=0, column=0)
        self.name_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.name_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Contact Info:").grid(row=1, column=0)
        self.contact_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.contact_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Skills (comma-separated):").grid(row=2, column=0)
        self.skills_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.skills_entry.grid(row=2, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Achievements (comma-separated):").grid(row=3, column=0)
        self.achievements_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.achievements_entry.grid(row=3, column=1)
        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=4, columnspan=2)
    def generate_and_save(self):
        name = self.name_entry.get()
        contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()
        skills = self.skills_entry.get().split(',')
        achievements = self.achievements_entry.get().split(',')
        if not name or not contact_info or not skills or not achievements:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please fill in all fields.")
            return
        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements)
        resume_content = resume_generator.generate_resume()
        # Save as PDF and Word
        resume_generator.save_as_pdf("resume.pdf")
        resume_generator.save_as_word("resume.docx")
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", "Resume generated successfully!")
```

'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document  # Ensure that the 'python-docx' package is installed
class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements
    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content
    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)
    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.save(filename)

resume_generator.py
```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document  # Ensure that the 'python-docx' package is installed
class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements
    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content
    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)
    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.save(filename)
```

Main entry point for the resume writing service application.

    root = Tk()

resume_generator.py
```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document
class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements
    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content
    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)
    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.save(filename)
```

gui.py
```python
'''
This module contains the GUI class that creates the graphical user interface
for the resume writing service application.
'''
from tkinter import Frame, Label, Entry, Button, Text, messagebox
from resume_generator import ResumeGenerator
class GUI:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Resume Writing Service")
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        Label(self.master, text="Name:").grid(row=0, column=0)
        self.name_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.name_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Contact Info:").grid(row=1, column=0)
        self.contact_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.contact_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Skills (comma-separated):").grid(row=2, column=0)
        self.skills_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.skills_entry.grid(row=2, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Achievements (comma-separated):").grid(row=3, column=0)
        self.achievements_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.achievements_entry.grid(row=3, column=1)
        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=4, columnspan=2)
    def generate_and_save(self):
        name = self.name_entry.get()
        contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()
        skills = self.skills_entry.get().split(',')
        achievements = self.achievements_entry.get().split(',')
        if not name or not contact_info or not skills or not achievements:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please fill in all fields.")
            return
        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements)
        resume_content = resume_generator.generate_resume()
        # Save as PDF and Word
        resume_generator.save_as_pdf("resume.pdf")
        resume_generator.save_as_word("resume.docx")
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", "Resume generated successfully!")
```

resume_generator.py
```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document
class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements
    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content
    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)
    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.save(filename)
```
gui.py
```python
'''
This module contains the GUI class that creates the graphical user interface
for the resume writing service application.
'''
from tkinter import Frame, Label, Entry, Button, Text, messagebox
from resume_generator import ResumeGenerator
class GUI:
    def __init__(self, master):
        self.master = master
        self.master.title("Resume Writing Service")
        self.create_widgets()
    def create_widgets(self):
        Label(self.master, text="Name:").grid(row=0, column=0)
        self.name_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.name_entry.grid(row=0, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Contact Info:").grid(row=1, column=0)
        self.contact_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.contact_entry.grid(row=1, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Skills (comma-separated):").grid(row=2, column=0)
        self.skills_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.skills_entry.grid(row=2, column=1)
        Label(self.master, text="Achievements (comma-separated):").grid(row=3, column=0)
        self.achievements_entry = Entry(self.master)
        self.achievements_entry.grid(row=3, column=1)
        Button(self.master, text="Generate Resume", command=self.generate_and_save).grid(row=4, columnspan=2)
    def generate_and_save(self):
        name = self.name_entry.get()
        contact_info = self.contact_entry.get()
        skills = self.skills_entry.get().split(',')
        achievements = self.achievements_entry.get().split(',')
        if not name or not contact_info or not skills or not achievements:
            messagebox.showerror("Input Error", "Please fill in all fields.")
            return
        resume_generator = ResumeGenerator(name, contact_info, skills, achievements)
        resume_content = resume_generator.generate_resume()
        # Save as PDF and Word
        resume_generator.save_as_pdf("resume.pdf")
        resume_generator.save_as_word("resume.docx")
        messagebox.showinfo("Success", "Resume generated successfully!")
```

resume_generator.py
```python
'''
This module contains the ResumeGenerator class that handles the creation
and saving of resumes in different formats.
'''
from fpdf import FPDF
from docx import Document
class ResumeGenerator:
    def __init__(self, name, contact_info, skills, achievements):
        self.name = name
        self.contact_info = contact_info
        self.skills = skills
        self.achievements = achievements
    def generate_resume(self):
        resume_content = f"Name: {self.name}\nContact Info: {self.contact_info}\n\nSkills:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.skills) + "\n\nAchievements:\n"
        resume_content += "\n".join(self.achievements)
        return resume_content
    def save_as_pdf(self, filename):
        pdf = FPDF()
        pdf.add_page()
        pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
        pdf.multi_cell(0, 10, self.generate_resume())
        pdf.output(filename)
    def save_as_word(self, filename):
        doc = Document()
        doc.add_heading(self.name, level=1)
        doc.add_paragraph(self.contact_info)
        doc.add_heading('Skills', level=2)
        for skill in self.skills:
            doc.add_paragraph(skill.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.add_heading('Achievements', level=2)
        for achievement in self.achievements:
            doc.add_paragraph(achievement.strip())  # Strip whitespace
        doc.save(filename)
```

# LangChain

Building applications with LLMs through composability

## Quick Install

`pip install langchain`

or

`conda install langchain -c conda-forge`

## 🤔 What is this?

Large language models (LLMs) are emerging as a transformative technology, enabling developers to build applications that they previously could not. However, using these LLMs in isolation is often insufficient for creating a truly powerful app - the real power comes when you can combine them with other sources of computation or knowledge.

This library aims to assist in the development of those types of applications. Common examples of these applications include:

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: Question Answering over Notion Database

**🤖 Agents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: GPT+WolframAlpha

- Getting started (installation, setting up the environment, simple examples)

```markdown
# Resume Writing Service

Create polished, ATS-friendly resumes for Network/RF Engineers, emphasizing achievements and skills in Python automation.

## Main Functions

- **Resume Generation**: Input personal details, skills, and achievements to generate a professional resume.
- **Output Formats**: Save the generated resume in both PDF and Word formats.
- **User-Friendly Interface**: A simple graphical user interface (GUI) for easy input and resume generation.

## Quick Install

To run the resume writing service, you need to install the necessary Python packages. You can do this using pip:

```bash
pip install fpdf python-docx
```

## 🤔 What is this?

This software is designed to help Network/RF Engineers create a professional resume that highlights their skills and achievements, particularly in Python automation. The generated resumes are ATS-friendly, ensuring they pass through Applicant Tracking Systems effectively.

## 📖 How to Use

1. **Run the Application**:
   - Execute the `main.py` file to launch the application.
   ```bash
   python main.py
   ```

2. **Input Your Information**:
   - Fill in the following fields in the GUI:
     - **Name**: Your full name.
     - **Contact Info**: Your email address and/or phone number.
     - **Skills**: List your skills related to Network/RF Engineering and Python automation, separated by commas.
     - **Achievements**: List your notable achievements, separated by commas.

3. **Generate the Resume**:
   - Click the "Generate Resume" button after filling in all fields.
   - If any fields are left empty, an error message will prompt you to fill them in.

4. **Output Files**:
   - Upon successful generation, the resume will be saved as `resume.pdf` and `resume.docx` in the same directory as the application.

5. **Optional LinkedIn Summary**:
   - While the current version does not automatically generate a LinkedIn summary, you can use the skills and achievements listed in your resume to craft a compelling summary for your LinkedIn profile.

## Additional Notes

- Ensure you have Python installed on your machine. This software is compatible with Python 3.x.
- The generated resumes are designed to be ATS-friendly, meaning they are structured in a way that Applicant Tracking Systems can easily read and parse the information.

## Support

For any issues or questions, please reach out to our support team via email at support@chatdev.com.

```

```markdown
# Resume Writing Service

Create polished, ATS-friendly resumes for Network/RF Engineers, emphasizing achievements and skills in Python automation.

## Main Functions

- **Resume Generation**: Input personal details, skills, and achievements to generate a professional resume.
- **Output Formats**: Save the generated resume in both PDF and Word formats.
- **User-Friendly Interface**: A simple graphical user interface (GUI) for easy input and resume generation.

## Quick Install

To run the resume writing service, you need to install the necessary Python packages. You can do this using pip:

```bash
pip install fpdf python-docx
```

## 🤔 What is this?

This software is designed to help Network/RF Engineers create a professional resume that highlights their skills and achievements, particularly in Python automation. The generated resumes are ATS-friendly, ensuring they pass through Applicant Tracking Systems effectively.

## 📖 How to Use

1. **Run the Application**:
   - Execute the `main.py` file to launch the application.
   ```bash
   python main.py
   ```

2. **Input Your Information**:
   - Fill in the following fields in the GUI:
     - **Name**: Your full name.
     - **Contact Info**: Your email address and/or phone number.
     - **Skills**: List your skills related to Network/RF Engineering and Python automation, separated by commas.
     - **Achievements**: List your notable achievements, separated by commas.

3. **Generate the Resume**:
   - Click the "Generate Resume" button after filling in all fields.
   - If any fields are left empty, an error message will prompt you to fill them in.

4. **Output Files**:
   - Upon successful generation, the resume will be saved as `resume.pdf` and `resume.docx` in the same directory as the application.

5. **Optional LinkedIn Summary**:
   - While the current version does not automatically generate a LinkedIn summary, you can use the skills and achievements listed in your resume to craft a compelling summary for your LinkedIn profile.

## Additional Notes

- Ensure you have Python installed on your machine. This software is compatible with Python 3.x.
- The generated resumes are designed to be ATS-friendly, meaning they are structured in a way that Applicant Tracking Systems can easily read and parse the information.

## Support

For any issues or questions, please reach out to our support team via email at support@chatdev.com.

```
